Select.Active.value = 0;
Clock.Polarity.value = 0;
Clock.Phase.value = 0;

Clock.Frequency.value = 50e6;

if(Clock.Frequency.value > 50e6) Clock.Frequency.value = 50e6;

DQ1.enable = false;
DQ2.enable = false;
DQ3.enable = false;

var GC9A01A_SLPIN = 0x10;  ///< Enter Sleep Mode
var GC9A01A_SLPOUT = 0x11; ///< Sleep Out
var GC9A01A_PTLON = 0x12;  ///< Partial Mode ON
var GC9A01A_NORON = 0x13;  ///< Normal Display Mode ON

var GC9A01A_INVOFF = 0x20;   ///< Display Inversion OFF
var GC9A01A_INVON = 0x21;    ///< Display Inversion ON
var GC9A01A_DISPOFF = 0x28;  ///< Display OFF
var GC9A01A_DISPON = 0x29;   ///< Display ON

var GC9A01A_CASET = 0x2A; ///< Column Address Set
var GC9A01A_PASET = 0x2B; ///< Page Address Set
var GC9A01A_RAMWR = 0x2C; ///< Memory Write

var GC9A01A_PTLAR = 0x30;    ///< Partial Area
var GC9A01A_VSCRDEF = 0x33;  ///< Vertical Scrolling Definition
var GC9A01A_TEOFF = 0x34;    ///< Tearing effect line off
var GC9A01A_TEON = 0x35;     ///< Tearing effect line on
var GC9A01A_MADCTL = 0x36;   ///< Memory Access Control
var GC9A01A_VSCRSADD = 0x37; ///< Vertical Scrolling Start Address
var GC9A01A_PIXFMT = 0x3A;   ///< COLMOD: Pixel Format Set

var GC9A01A1_DFUNCTR = 0xB6; ///< Display Function Control

var GC9A01A1_VREG1A = 0xC3; ///< Vreg1a voltage control
var GC9A01A1_VREG1B = 0xC4; ///< Vreg1b voltage control
var GC9A01A1_VREG2A = 0xC9; ///< Vreg2a voltage control

var GC9A01A_RDID1 = 0xDA; ///< Read ID 1
var GC9A01A_RDID2 = 0xDB; ///< Read ID 2
var GC9A01A_RDID3 = 0xDC; ///< Read ID 3

var GC9A01A1_GMCTRP1 = 0xE0; ///< Positive Gamma Correction
var GC9A01A1_GMCTRN1 = 0xE1; ///< Negative Gamma Correction
var GC9A01A_FRAMERATE = 0xE8; ///< Frame rate control

var GC9A01A_INREGEN2 = 0xEF; ///< Inter register enable 2
var GC9A01A_GAMMA1 = 0xF0; ///< Set gamma 1
var GC9A01A_GAMMA2 = 0xF1; ///< Set gamma 2
var GC9A01A_GAMMA3 = 0xF2; ///< Set gamma 3
var GC9A01A_GAMMA4 = 0xF3; ///< Set gamma 4

var GC9A01A_INREGEN1 = 0xFE; ///< Inter register enable 1

var MADCTL_MY = 0x80;  ///< Bottom to top
var MADCTL_MX = 0x40;  ///< Right to left
var MADCTL_MV = 0x20;  ///< Reverse Mode
var MADCTL_ML = 0x10;  ///< LCD refresh Bottom to top
var MADCTL_RGB = 0x00; ///< Red-Green-Blue pixel order
var MADCTL_BGR = 0x08; ///< Blue-Green-Red pixel order
var MADCTL_MH = 0x04;  ///< LCD refresh right to left

// var DISPLAY_WIDTH         DT_INST_PROP(0, width)
// var DISPLAY_HEIGHT        DT_INST_PROP(0, height)

// Command codes:
var COL_ADDR_SET =       0x2A;
var ROW_ADDR_SET =       0x2B;
var MEM_WR =             0x2C;
var MEM_WR_CONT =        0x3C;
var COLOR_MODE =         0x3A;
var COLOR_MODE_12_BIT = 0x03;
var COLOR_MODE_16_BIT = 0x05;
var COLOR_MODE_18_BIT = 0x06;
var SLPIN =              0x10;
var SLPOUT =             0x11;

function writeCmd(cmd, data)
{
    DIO.Set(3, 1);
    DIO.Set(3, 0);
    Write(8, [cmd]);
    if(data.length > 0)
    {
        DIO.Set(3, 1);
        Write(8, data);
    }
    DIO.Set(3, 0);
}

function init()
{
    DIO.Set(4, 0);
    DIO.Set(4, 1);
    
    DIO.Set(3, 0);
    
    writeCmd(GC9A01A_INREGEN2, []);
    writeCmd(0xEB, [0x14]);
    writeCmd(GC9A01A_INREGEN1, []);
    writeCmd(GC9A01A_INREGEN2, []);
    writeCmd(0xEB, [0x14]);
    writeCmd(0x84, [0x40]);
    writeCmd(0x85, [0xFF]);
    writeCmd(0x86, [0xFF]);
    writeCmd(0x87, [0xFF]);
    writeCmd(0x88, [0x0A]);
    writeCmd(0x89, [0x21]);
    writeCmd(0x8A, [0x00]);
    writeCmd(0x8B, [0x80]);
    writeCmd(0x8C, [0x01]);
    writeCmd(0x8D, [0x01]);
    writeCmd(0x8E, [0xFF]);
    writeCmd(0x8F, [0xFF]);
    writeCmd(0xB6, [0x00, 0x00]);
    writeCmd(GC9A01A_MADCTL, [MADCTL_MH | MADCTL_MY | 0 | MADCTL_BGR]);
    writeCmd(GC9A01A_PIXFMT, [COLOR_MODE_16_BIT]);
    writeCmd(0x90, [0x08, 0x08, 0x08, 0x08]);
    writeCmd(0xBD, [0x06]);
    writeCmd(0xBC, [0x00]);
    writeCmd(0xFF, [0x60, 0x01, 0x04]);
    writeCmd(GC9A01A1_VREG1A, [0x13]);
    writeCmd(GC9A01A1_VREG1B, [0x13]);
    writeCmd(GC9A01A1_VREG2A, [0x22]);
    writeCmd(0xBE, [0x11]);
    writeCmd(GC9A01A1_GMCTRN1, [0x10, 0x0E]);
    writeCmd(0xDF, [0x21, 0x0c, 0x02]);
    writeCmd(GC9A01A_GAMMA1, [0x45, 0x09, 0x08, 0x08, 0x26, 0x2A]);
    writeCmd(GC9A01A_GAMMA2, [0x43, 0x70, 0x72, 0x36, 0x37, 0x6F]);
    writeCmd(GC9A01A_GAMMA3, [0x45, 0x09, 0x08, 0x08, 0x26, 0x2A]);
    writeCmd(GC9A01A_GAMMA4, [0x43, 0x70, 0x72, 0x36, 0x37, 0x6F]);
    writeCmd(0xED, [0x1B, 0x0B]);
    writeCmd(0xAE, [0x77]);
    writeCmd(0xCD, [0x63]);
    writeCmd(0x70, [0x07, 0x07, 0x04, 0x0E, 0x0F, 0x09, 0x07, 0x08, 0x03]);
    writeCmd(GC9A01A_FRAMERATE, [0x34]);
    writeCmd(0x62, [0x18, 0x0D, 0x71, 0xED, 0x70, 0x70, 0x18, 0x0F, 0x71, 0xEF, 0x70, 0x70]);
    writeCmd(0x63, [0x18, 0x11, 0x71, 0xF1, 0x70, 0x70, 0x18, 0x13, 0x71, 0xF3, 0x70, 0x70]);
    writeCmd(0x64, [0x28, 0x29, 0xF1, 0x01, 0xF1, 0x00, 0x07]);
    writeCmd(0x66, [0x3C, 0x00, 0xCD, 0x67, 0x45, 0x45, 0x10, 0x00, 0x00, 0x00]);
    writeCmd(0x67, [0x00, 0x3C, 0x00, 0x00, 0x00, 0x01, 0x54, 0x10, 0x32, 0x98]);
    writeCmd(0x74, [0x10, 0x85, 0x80, 0x00, 0x00, 0x4E, 0x00]);
    writeCmd(0x98, [0x3e, 0x07]);
    writeCmd(GC9A01A_TEON, [GC9A01A_INVOFF]);
    writeCmd(GC9A01A_INVON, []);
    writeCmd(GC9A01A_DISPOFF, []);
    writeCmd(GC9A01A_SLPOUT, []);
}

function setFrame()
{
    var start_x = 0;
    var start_y = 0;
    var end_x = 240 - 1;
    var end_y = 240 - 1;
    data = [];
    data[0] = (start_x >> 8) & 0xFF;
    data[1] = start_x & 0xFF;
    data[2] = (end_x >> 8) & 0xFF;
    data[3] = end_x & 0xFF;
    writeCmd(COL_ADDR_SET, data);

    data[0] = (start_y >> 8) & 0xFF;
    data[1] = start_y & 0xFF;
    data[2] = (end_y >> 8) & 0xFF;
    data[3] = end_y & 0xFF;
    writeCmd(ROW_ADDR_SET, data);
}

function rgb8_to_rgb565(r, g, b)
{
    var red5 = round(r / 255 * 31);
    var gre5 = round(g / 255 * 63);
    var blu5 = round(b / 255 * 31);
    return ((red5 << 11) | (gre5 << 5) | blu5);
}

function writeData(data)
{
    setFrame();
    DIO.Set(3, 1);
    DIO.Set(3, 0);
    Write(8, [GC9A01A_RAMWR]);
    var divisor = 240;
    DIO.Set(3, 1);
    for(var i = 0; i < data.length / divisor; i++)
    {
        var idx = i * divisor;
        Write(8, data.slice(idx, idx + divisor));
    }
    DIO.Set(3, 0);
}

function clearColor(r,g,b)
{
    setFrame();
    DIO.Set(3, 1);
    DIO.Set(3, 0);
    Write(8, [GC9A01A_RAMWR]);
    var color = rgb8_to_rgb565(r, g, b);
    var colorh = (color >> 8) & 0xFF;
    var colorl = color & 0xFF;
    var data = Array();
    for(var i = 0; i < 240*240; i++)
    {
        data.push(colorh);
        data.push(colorl);
    }
    var divisor = 240;
    DIO.Set(3, 1);
    for(var i = 0; i < data.length / divisor; i++)
    {
        var idx = i * divisor;
        Write(8, data.slice(idx, idx + divisor));
    }
    DIO.Set(3, 0);
}


init();
clearColor(0, 0, 0);
writeCmd(GC9A01A_DISPON, []);
clearColor(0, 128, 98);
